        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2319163182" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13153093681658495550"><br/><b>Review :</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1554272533ra/27307417.gif' width='450' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Honestly, I think all my opinions on this book could be summed with that one gif above. <br/><br/>But do you get what it means?<br/><br/>No?<br/><br/>Same.<br/><br/>I think it's time to call it quits with this series. I wasn't pleased with Restore Me as it didn't really offer anything plot wise, but fuck, you give me Daddy Warner, I'll give you my soul (and my money)<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1554272533ra/27307418.gif' width='450' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So I decided, ah, fuck it. Maybe Tahereh just need to get into the groove of writing the series again after so many years. I gave it the benefit of the doubt and w</span>
  <span id="freeText13153093681658495550" style="display:none"><br><b>Review :</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1554272533ra/27307417.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, I think all my opinions on this book could be summed with that one gif above. <br><br>But do you get what it means?<br><br>No?<br><br>Same.<br><br>I think it's time to call it quits with this series. I wasn't pleased with Restore Me as it didn't really offer anything plot wise, but fuck, you give me Daddy Warner, I'll give you my soul (and my money)<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1554272533ra/27307418.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So I decided, ah, fuck it. Maybe Tahereh just need to get into the groove of writing the series again after so many years. I gave it the benefit of the doubt and went into Defy Me. <br><br>Now, was it bad? No, not really. <br><br>Did it exceed my expectations? Hard to say, since I had none going into this one.<br><br>Would I continue down this series? Maybe, hard to say. <br><br>All there is in this book was a shit ton of flashbacks that could have been told in a page, and –– wait for it –– a fuck ton of crying.<br><br>Because who doesn't just fucking squee at the thought of reading girls crying. Hmm? Got me going just thinking about it, oh definitely.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1554272534ra/27307419.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not to mention, it felt like we were regressing? At the end of book 3, Juliette was this strong woman that could stand up for herself and let nothing bring her down. But then in book 4 and 5, the bitch fucking went downhill and reverted back to book 1 Juliette all over again.<br><br>I mean, <i>bitch</i>, if I wanted to experience crying, babbling Juliette all over again, I could have just re-read the first two books. I don't got to spend money to buy two more book just to read more on that. <br><br>Another thing, Warner. Look, I enjoy Tahereh and her writing. But dude, what the fuck have you done with my baby? In the first 3 books, he was this level headed, strong, cold but caring guy. As the series progresses, why does he slowly becoming a love-sick puppy? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380433712ra/873001.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Which leads me to think that, Shatter Me series should have stopped at book 3. Reading book 4 and 5, makes it feels as if Tahereh has just ran out of ideas, and are just milking this series for money. <br><br><br>------------------------------------------------------------------<br><br><br><b>Fangirl Episode Prior to reading : </b> <br><br>Hi.<br><br>I...uh....just finished Restore Me. <br><br>And...uh...I...uh...kind of need this book...like....RIGHT NOW? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1512969155ra/24651986.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520390705ra/25173284.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1520390789ra/25173286.gif" width="450" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/420316.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b> Blog : <a href="http://literaturesandmovies.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Click here for more of my reviews</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13153093681658495550" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2328375696" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2328375696" />
    <a title="Tara ☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26094436-tara"><img alt="Tara ☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599527456p2/26094436.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2328375696?book_show_action=true">Jan 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tara ☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tara ☽" href="/user/show/26094436-tara">Tara ☽</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26094436-tara?shelf=awesome-hero">awesome-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26094436-tara?shelf=favourites-2019">favourites-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26094436-tara?shelf=oh-the-feelings">oh-the-feelings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26094436-tara?shelf=ultimate-otps">ultimate-otps</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26094436-tara?shelf=superpowers">superpowers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26094436-tara?shelf=action">action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26094436-tara?shelf=awesome-heroine">awesome-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26094436-tara?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26094436-tara?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2328375696" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer380267462326836026"><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Hello, my name is Tara, and I'm starting a support group for Shatter Me stans.</b><br/><br/>Honestly, after the mess that was <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34992929.Restore_Me__Shatter_Me___4_' title='Restore Me (Shatter Me, #4) by Tahereh Mafi' rel='nofollow noopener'>Restore Me</a>, it's probably an understatement to say I was nervous for this book. I was terrified that the story and characters that are so beloved to me would be damaged beyond repair, until they were so unrecognisable from what I used to hold so dear that my memory of this series would be forever tainted.<br/><br/>Now that I've read it, I'm going on the record to say I should have trusted</span>
  <span id="freeText380267462326836026" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Hello, my name is Tara, and I'm starting a support group for Shatter Me stans.</b><br /><br />Honestly, after the mess that was <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34992929.Restore_Me__Shatter_Me___4_" title="Restore Me (Shatter Me, #4) by Tahereh Mafi" rel="nofollow noopener">Restore Me</a>, it's probably an understatement to say I was nervous for this book. I was terrified that the story and characters that are so beloved to me would be damaged beyond repair, until they were so unrecognisable from what I used to hold so dear that my memory of this series would be forever tainted.<br /><br />Now that I've read it, I'm going on the record to say I should have trusted dear Ms Mafi. She knows her characters better than any of us do, and she indeed knows what she's doing. I still stand by the fact that Restore Me was rather a mess, but now I understand that the events of that book were necessary to get to where we are now. I think that, just like with the original trilogy, the books of this second arc cannot be examined in isolation. The first trilogy was one overarching story split into three books, and the same can be said for the second one. It's probably easier to think of it as one story rather than three separate books, because that's really what it is. It's one story chopped into three, for good or for ill.<br /><br />My biggest fear with this book was how things would go down with Warner and Juliette - or should I say <b>Ella</b>. (Not gonna lie, I'm probably always going to think of her as Juliette, because I spent 6 years thinking of her that way and it's too late to change now lol.) I'm happy to say that my OTP is back on top form in this book, especially in light of the little blip in the last book. In fact, they almost act as if the fight in Restore Me never happened, which is good because I like to think of it that way too. There are quite a few enormous revelations in this book regarding Warner and Juliette/Ella and I'm going to be honest and say I don't think everyone's going to like them. I personally loved the developments we got here, just because I'm a massive sucker for the 'tragic/star-crossed lovers/soul mates' storyline and this book provided some EXCELLENCE on that front.<br /><br />Also an amazing scene involving a shower that, let's just say, made ME need a shower after I'd read it. A very cold one. <b>*wink*</b><br /><br />Honestly, the title of this book should probably be changed to <b>Plot Twist: The Novel</b>. There are so many revelations that completely alter your entire perception of this story, including the events of the original trilogy. Again, I do think that this is something that not everybody will like, but I personally loved it because, in my opinion, everything made more sense. It answered many of the questions I was left with after the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13188676.Ignite_Me__Shatter_Me___3_" title="Ignite Me (Shatter Me, #3) by Tahereh Mafi" rel="nofollow noopener">Ignite Me</a>, and erased that strangely 'convenient' feeling of the plot of the first three books. The world of this series feels so much larger now, so much more expansive and interesting. The stakes are so much higher now. The events of the original trilogy feel like child's play compared to the enormity of what our characters are facing now.<br /><br />I will say that much of this book reminded me of the oft-dreaded 'middle trilogy book'. It was very much a tale of characters getting from Point A to Point B, setting all the pieces in place for the grand finale. I didn't mind as much because the way it went about was so interesting, and I was so invested in all the revelations and character moments. Again, this is another example of the fact that this second trilogy can only be appreciated in full once all the books are out, and it can be read as one larger story. I don't see that as a drawback, just something that readers might want to be conscious of. <br /><br />My favourite POV was definitely Warner's. I adore being inside that boy's head. He is so intelligent and his backstory just constantly breaks my heart. There were so many moments in this book where I was so, so proud of him. He's come so far since the lonely, broken boy he once was and I just wanted to constantly tell him 'Darling you're doing so well'. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I was honestly YODELLING when he stabbed his father in the neck. Anyone else remember that boy who was constantly raising a gun to his abusive father and constantly breaking down, unable to do it? Yeah, me too. He's come so far.<br /><br />Speaking of which, of all the characters to be protected by plot armour, why does it have to be freaking Anderson? The guy is practically indestructible. He's been shot multiple times, had his feet literally ripped off his ankles, beaten, stabbed in the neck, yet he still manages to survive? Are you kidding me? Can the guy just stay dead pls? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />The other characters were wonderful too (except the side characters remain, sadly, slightly underdeveloped), but Warner is and will always be the standout for me. He was the reason I kept reading back in the original trilogy when I was constantly frustrated by Juliette and Adam. Kenji was another reason that kept me reading, but Warner was always my favourite. Always, always. He's basically become the archetype for 'villain who was secretly the hero all along' in YA, and I'm so happy for that. He was the original. He is the one to which we compare all others. And nobody will ever be able to measure up.<br /><br />I still have many questions, and I do think there were some slightly strange decisions made. For example, many important conversations take place off-page, and then we have to hear about them second-hand, which I thought was a bit odd. And it felt very much like the middle of a larger story arc, rather than a story in of itself, but I've already talked about that.<br /><br />Now all I have to do is twiddle my thumbs and await the grand finale.</span>
  <a data-text-id="380267462326836026" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2478735445" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2478735445" />
    <a title="Nouha Aouine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/59336578-nouha-aouine"><img alt="Nouha Aouine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1602602548p2/59336578.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2478735445?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nouha Aouine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nouha Aouine" href="/user/show/59336578-nouha-aouine">Nouha Aouine</a>

<div id="review_1983149386" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1983149386" />
    <a title="Sam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/63175440-sam"><img alt="Sam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585865739p2/63175440.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1983149386?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sam" href="/user/show/63175440-sam">Sam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/63175440-sam?shelf=read-in-2019">read-in-2019</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1983149386" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5836676515399538637">Lowering my rating from 2.5 to 1.5. I’ve been thinking, and I'm just mad at this point because Tahereh Mafi took everything that was canon from the original trilogy and just tore it apart. And I spent money on this thing so there’s that too.<br/><br/>Review:<br/><br/>Welcome to 2019, the year where almost all of my most anticipated releases have let me down in some way, some more than others!<br/><br/>I am just so disappointed. I was expecting so much more from this. The title, the cover, the synopsis...all of these things m</span>
  <span id="freeText5836676515399538637" style="display:none">Lowering my rating from 2.5 to 1.5. I’ve been thinking, and I'm just mad at this point because Tahereh Mafi took everything that was canon from the original trilogy and just tore it apart. And I spent money on this thing so there’s that too.<br /><br />Review:<br /><br />Welcome to 2019, the year where almost all of my most anticipated releases have let me down in some way, some more than others!<br /><br />I am just so disappointed. I was expecting so much more from this. The title, the cover, the synopsis...all of these things made it sound like this book was going to be epic. And, it just...wasn't.<br /><br />Kenji did not need a POV in this. It added literally added nothing to the story except filling in what would have been a few gaps. Ha. As if there weren't enough of those.<br /><br />The ENTIRE time I read this book, I was confused. For all 357 pages, I did not understand what was happening. And I thought, is it me? Am I not remembering things and reading correctly? But no. I've come to the conclusion that this book was just a bit of a mess.<br /><br />Most of it is told in memories for like the first 200 PAGES. TWO HUNDRED. And major info dumps were just thrown in all at once. So you could see why this is confusing. There is new information just being loaded onto the reader all at once, and they're trying to figure out what the hell is going on with the memories and stuff. <br /><br />Another thing I didn't love was something that seems to be a new thing for popular YA authors. No spoilers but...If you've read this you can probably guess. Leigh Bardugo, Cassandra Clare, and now Tahereh Mafi...yikes. Let's stop doing this trope, please, no one likes it.<br /><br />Um, also. The title and cover and synopsis all made it seem like this book was going to be insane and there was going to be BATTLE. That stuff would get DONE. I think there was probably one action scene in the whole book, and it felt like very little was accomplished in terms of plot.<br /><br />Kenji and Nazeera’s relationship also felt so unnatural and sudden in this book. Like ??? And Nazeera had like zero characterization in this, not gonna lie. Which is a sham because I liked her in Restore Me.<br /><br />Also, in my original review I put up here, I said I liked the ending, but thinking now, it was like fan fiction and not in a good way. So, nope.<br /><br />I did like that one part, when Juliette *spoiler* *spoiler*. My mouth dropped open in awe. <br /><br />The friendships are another thing I really like about this book., although I wish we’d gotten a bit more time with them.<br /><br />Overall, after Restore Me, maybe my expectations were too high. I just don't understand how it went from my favourite book in the series to my least favourite so quickly. Let's hope the rest of my anticipated 2019 serve me greatness, as Bloodwitch and Priory have.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5836676515399538637" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12402009-alana?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2620745015" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10958026174822244202"><b>
  <i>"Today is not forever. Happiness does not happen. Happiness must be uncovered, separated from the skin of pain. It must be claimed."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Believe me, no one is more disappointed than me about this rating, even if I am a few months late on picking this up. But this....just felt so off compared to the first four books. I should have known what was coming though, when things went downhill with Kenji's novella. If I'm being honest this also felt more like reading fan-fiction rather than reading the ne</span>
  <span id="freeText10958026174822244202" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Today is not forever. Happiness does not happen. Happiness must be uncovered, separated from the skin of pain. It must be claimed."</i>
</b><br /><br />Believe me, no one is more disappointed than me about this rating, even if I am a few months late on picking this up. But this....just felt so off compared to the first four books. I should have known what was coming though, when things went downhill with Kenji's novella. If I'm being honest this also felt more like reading fan-fiction rather than reading the next book in the Shatter Me series #sorrynotsorry. And I really hate to say this but I'd by lying if I didn't, this should have stayed a trilogy.<br /><br />Here's the thing, a lot of people who originally read the first three books didn't care for <em>Restore Me</em> when it came out. Whether it be the wait was too long and Warner and Juliette just didn't hold the same interest to them, or they felt it was unnecessary, some readers complained that it was just too much too late. Me though? I <strong>LOVED</strong> <em>Restore Me, </em>but I also binged this entire series for the first time one week prior to <em>Restore Me's</em> release and could not wait to get my hands on it so that's probably why. I just couldn't believe all the new information we got in that book and then with that cliffhanger of an ending I was so excited for <em>Defy Me</em>. However, this book definitely just felt like even more of an info dump than <em>Restore Me</em> and not in a good way.<br /><br />The problem now is that between <em>Restore Me</em> and <em>Defy Me</em> there are so many things that were added to the story that came completely out of left field, how they're all going to be wrapped up in the last book is beyond me. Obviously I'm still going to pick it up to find out how it ends, but I am extremely skeptical as to how this series is going to get a wrap up that feels neat and complete. Reading this felt like the author was literally just throwing twists and turns into the story for the hell of it and this is not the Tahereh Mafi I'm used to. It was such a weird reading experience because it was a quick read and I was happy to be back with my favorites but it just felt all wrong at the same time. I will always ship Juliette and Warner (yes, I'm still calling her Juliette) and Kenji will always be one of my favorite wittiest characters, but otherwise to keep things nice and simple...<strong>THIS AIN'T IT. </strong><br /><br /><a href="https://thebookishchicksblog.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookishchick" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebookishchick_/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10958026174822244202" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2688819553" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2688819553" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44125660-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600268807p2/44125660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2688819553?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/44125660-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781405291798" href="/book/show/43287829-defy-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=book-series">book-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=characters-i-loved">characters-i-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=nice-enough">nice-enough</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=2019-reads">2019-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2688819553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1501418030363195014"><b>2.5 Stars!</b><br/><br/>I know I'm in the minority here, but <i>honestly</i> I really didn't see the point of this book. I'm not going to lie, when I saw Kenji had a POV I was so excited to see what was to come, but I can't even begin to explain.<br/><br/><b>Spoilers ahead please be aware, I just have too many questions!</b><br/><br/>There just seemed to be so many "twists and turns" but with this I was just bored by it. Too many tropes that didn't need to be included and not only that, but so much of it was unexplained it kind of left me fru</span>
  <span id="freeText1501418030363195014" style="display:none"><b>2.5 Stars!</b><br /><br />I know I'm in the minority here, but <i>honestly</i> I really didn't see the point of this book. I'm not going to lie, when I saw Kenji had a POV I was so excited to see what was to come, but I can't even begin to explain.<br /><br /><b>Spoilers ahead please be aware, I just have too many questions!</b><br /><br />There just seemed to be so many "twists and turns" but with this I was just bored by it. Too many tropes that didn't need to be included and not only that, but so much of it was unexplained it kind of left me frustrated by the end. I genuinely thought we'd have some answers as to what happened and if I missed them please can someone explain. In short the things that I don't understand are:<br />1. Memories, how on earth did they come back<br />2. The "revival" of a character<br />3. What the actual fuck happened to everyone and why was it only Kenji taken along with Warner and Juliette?<br />4. How, just how did they track a plane <u>on foot</u> and then manage to shoot it out of the sky?<br />5. Why was Nazeera with a certain someone?<br /><br />Edit - I think I’ve cleared up 3 of these points :)<br /><br />The things I <b>liked?</b><br />- I'm going to put this plainly, I fucking love Kenji with all my heart. For me, he is one of my favourite characters ever and he deserves the world! Just his constant support, trying to help, his love for Castle (my heart) he is forever a complete babe.<br />- I'm not gunna lie, I wasn't ever here for Juliette/Ella with any of the characters, but I can safely say this has well and truly won me over for her and Warner to be number one, I'm eating my words here because I <i>kind of</i> love their relationship, it clearly has its flaws, however what relationship doesn't? Not only that, the understanding, trust and love... god it was gooooood!<br />- Kenji asking Warner about all of the films he hadn't watched so amusing<br />- The amount of times I said what the fuck while reading this seriously makes me laugh<br /><br />Overall, I'm kind of disappointed but I'm going to continue on, I've come too far not to, I just hope it picks up because after the ending I <u>am</u> intrigued to see where this goes, but (once again I'm not 100% certain) if this is the last book how on earth is it all going to get wrapped up?!<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1900672973?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">Shatter Me</a> - 3 Stars<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2211828780?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">Unravel Me</a> - 4 Stars<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2216752546?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">Ignite Me</a>- 4.5 Stars<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2221431993" rel="nofollow noopener">Restore Me</a> - 4 Stars<br />Defy Me - 2.5 Stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="1501418030363195014" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OG2n2an62qvjpozOiEZ4BJb1L76UzeFr5zzl1I9D/z1P+YbLzrO+1BQYsSkXkdwmilgLCLNGMHrzl6MfLOP0Wg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HOj4THZvnePJTQ0W38NIJS1v0U32X1tOnYcEeChkzQ9rfNleESb5nD7zMPFAFOwHMcL1+9HUil+JLEKzi8TGaA==')})
  }
//]]>
